## 1: Prompt 1

Optimize the substrate kernel in /workspace/kernel_benchmark/kb_eval_pipeline/runs/kb1/p09/optimization_rounds_no_invariants/round1/output_model_new.py

Use MFMA instructions `S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32` to do matrix multiplications and loads the data from global memory using vectorized loads S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4. The MFMA instruction computes 32x32x8 matmul cooperatively in a wave. Build larger tiles by issuing multiple MFMA instructions across K and output subtiles.

Stage A and B through LDS. Each thread loads operand fragments in 16-byte chunks. Treat each 16-byte fragment as `(4, S.u32)` and reinterpret it as `2 x (4, S.bf16)`. Feed both `(4, S.bf16)` halves into MFMA in natural order. The intended effect is a cooperative `32x32x16` accumulation from two natural MFMA steps. Do not add lane-dependent or K-dependent control flow to select halves.
  - The two `(4, S.bf16)` halves from one 16-byte LDS load collectively represent a swizzled `32x16` operand contribution with 4-column interleaving.
  - Consuming them in natural order must produce the same final C as a naive conceptual layout because operand pairings remain consistent under MFMA swizzle.

Scale the kernel from one wave to four waves without changing the MFMA per-wave invariant. Interpret the 4 warps as a 2 x 2 warp grid. Keep MFMA math identical per warp. Only add warp ownership offsets at operand fetch and output writeback.

import torch
import torch.nn as nn

import substrate
import substrate.language as S


M = 32768
K = 32
N = 32768


@substrate.jit
def gemm_kernel(
    A: S.Tensor((32768, 32), S.bf16),
    B: S.Tensor((32, 32768), S.bf16),
    C: S.Tensor((32768, 32768), S.bf16),
):
    for i in S.range(M):
        for j in S.range(N):
            acc = S.convert(0.0, S.f32)
            for kk in S.range(K):
                acc += S.convert(A[i, kk], S.f32) * S.convert(B[kk, j], S.f32)
            C[i, j] = S.convert(acc, S.bf16)


class ModelNew(nn.Module):
    def __init__(self):
        super().__init__()

    def forward(self, A, B):
        if tuple(A.shape) != (32768, 32) or tuple(B.shape) != (32, 32768):
            return torch.matmul(A, B)
        A = A.contiguous()
        B = B.contiguous()
        C = torch.empty((32768, 32768), device=A.device, dtype=A.dtype)
        gemm_kernel[lambda: ((1, 1, 1), (1, 1, 1))](A, B, C)
        return C

#!/usr/bin/env python3
import unittest

import torch

import substrate
import substrate.language as S
from substrate.testing import has_rocm


@substrate.jit
def gemm_mfma_16x16x16(
    A: S.Tensor((64, 4), S.u32),
    B: S.Tensor((64, 4), S.u32),
    C: S.Tensor((64, 4), S.f32),
):
    lane = S.thread_id(0)

    c_lane = S.full((4,), 0.0, S.f32)

    m_a = S.view(A[lane], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.f16))
    m_b = S.view(B[lane], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.f16))

    c_lane = S.amdgpu.mfma_16x16x16_f16_f32(m_a[0], m_b[0], c_lane)
    c_lane = S.amdgpu.mfma_16x16x16_f16_f32(m_a[1], m_b[1], c_lane)

    C[lane] = c_lane


@substrate.jit
def gemm_mfma_32x32x8_bf16(
    A: S.Tensor((64, 2), S.u32),
    B: S.Tensor((64, 2), S.u32),
    C: S.Tensor((64, 16), S.f32),
):
    lane = S.thread_id(0)

    c_lane = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)

    m_a = S.view(A[lane], S.Tensor((1, 4, 1), S.bf16))
    m_b = S.view(B[lane], S.Tensor((1, 4, 1), S.bf16))

    c_lane = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(m_a[0], m_b[0], c_lane)

    C[lane] = c_lane

#!/usr/bin/env python3
import unittest

import torch

import substrate
import substrate.language as S
import _substrate_bindings as _C
from substrate.compiler.code_generator import (
    _build_import_module,
    _collect_jit_dependencies,
    _get_function_def,
)
from substrate.testing import has_rocm


@substrate.jit
def kernel_amdgpu_raw_buffer_roundtrip(
    src: S.Tensor((7,), S.i32),
    dst: S.Tensor((7,), S.i32),
    range_bytes: S.i32,
):
    src_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(src, range_bytes)
    dst_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(dst, range_bytes)

    zero = S.convert(0, S.i32)
    offset_x2 = S.convert(4, S.i32)
    offset_x4 = S.convert(12, S.i32)

    value_x1 = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x1(src_rsrc, zero, zero, 0)
    value_x2 = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x2(src_rsrc, zero, offset_x2, 0)
    value_x4 = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(src_rsrc, zero, offset_x4, 0)

    S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_store_x1(value_x1, dst_rsrc, zero, zero, 0)
    S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_store_x2(value_x2, dst_rsrc, zero, offset_x2, 0)
    S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_store_x4(value_x4, dst_rsrc, zero, offset_x4, 0)


@substrate.jit
def kernel_amdgpu_raw_buffer_bf16_view(
    src: S.Tensor((8,), S.bf16),
    dst: S.Tensor((8,), S.bf16),
    range_bytes: S.i32,
):
    src_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(src, range_bytes)

    zero = S.convert(0, S.i32)
    packed = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(src_rsrc, zero, zero, 0)
    frag = S.view(packed, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))

    for i in S.range(2):
        for j in S.range(4):
            dst[i * 4 + j] = frag[i, j, 0]


def generate_mlir(jit_fn) -> str:
    jit_deps = _collect_jit_dependencies(jit_fn)
    import_module = _build_import_module([jit_fn, *jit_deps])

    generator = _C.MLIRGenerator()
    generator.generate_from_python_ast(import_module)

    for dep in jit_deps:
        dep_func = _get_function_def(dep.parse())
        generator.visit_function_def(dep_func, "[]", "jit")

    kernel_func = _get_function_def(jit_fn.parse())
    generator.visit_function_def(kernel_func, "[]", "kernel")
    return generator.get_mlir()


@unittest.skipUnless(
    has_rocm(),
    "Requires ROCm/HIP with an AMD GPU.",
)
class TestAMDGPUBufferOps(unittest.TestCase):
    def test_raw_buffer_roundtrip(self):
        src = torch.arange(7, dtype=torch.int32, device="cuda") * 17 - 9
        dst = torch.full((7,), -1, dtype=torch.int32, device="cuda")
        range_bytes = src.numel() * src.element_size()

        kernel_amdgpu_raw_buffer_roundtrip[lambda: ((1, 1, 1), (1, 1, 1))](
            src, dst, range_bytes
        )

        self.assertTrue(
            torch.equal(dst.cpu(), src.cpu()),
            f"Expected: {src.tolist()}, Actual: {dst.tolist()}",
        )

    def test_make_rsrc_generates_pointer_and_range(self):
        mlir = generate_mlir(kernel_amdgpu_raw_buffer_roundtrip)

        self.assertIn(
            "substrate.memref.extract_aligned_pointer_as_index",
            mlir,
        )
        self.assertGreaterEqual(mlir.count("vector.insert %arg2"), 2, mlir)
        self.assertEqual(mlir.count("substrate.gpu.amdgpu_raw_buffer_load"), 3, mlir)
        self.assertEqual(mlir.count("substrate.gpu.amdgpu_raw_buffer_store"), 3, mlir)

    def test_raw_buffer_bf16_view_extract(self):
        src = torch.randn((8,), dtype=torch.bfloat16, device="cuda")
        dst = torch.zeros((8,), dtype=torch.bfloat16, device="cuda")
        range_bytes = src.numel() * src.element_size()

        kernel_amdgpu_raw_buffer_bf16_view[lambda: ((1, 1, 1), (1, 1, 1))](
            src, dst, range_bytes
        )

        self.assertTrue(
            torch.equal(dst.cpu(), src.cpu()),
            f"Expected: {src.tolist()}, Actual: {dst.tolist()}",
        )


if __name__ == "__main__":
    unittest.main()

#!/usr/bin/env python3
import unittest

import torch

import substrate
import substrate.language as S


@substrate.jit
def kernel_shm_basic(
    input_data: S.Tensor((32,), S.i32),
    output_data: S.Tensor((32,), S.i32),
):
    shared_buf = S.make_shared((32,), S.i32)

    thread_id = S.thread_id(0)

    shared_buf[thread_id] = input_data[thread_id]

    S.syncthreads()

    read_idx = (thread_id + 1) % 32
    output_data[thread_id] = shared_buf[read_idx]


@substrate.jit
def kernel_shm_2d(
    input_matrix: S.Tensor((16, 16), S.f32),
    output_matrix: S.Tensor((16, 16), S.f32),
):
    shared_buf = S.make_shared((16, 16), S.f32)

    thread_x = S.thread_id(0)
    thread_y = S.thread_id(1)

    shared_buf[thread_y, thread_x] = input_matrix[thread_y, thread_x]

    S.syncthreads()

    output_matrix[thread_y, thread_x] = shared_buf[thread_x, thread_y]  # Transpose


@substrate.jit
def kernel_shm_reduction(
    input_data: S.Tensor((32,), S.f32),
    result: S.Tensor((2,), S.f32),
):
    shared_buf = S.make_shared((32,), S.f32)

    thread_id = S.thread_id(0)

    shared_buf[thread_id] = input_data[thread_id]
    S.syncthreads()

    stride = 16
    for i in S.range(5):  # log2(32) = 5
        if thread_id < stride:
            shared_buf[thread_id] = shared_buf[thread_id] + shared_buf[thread_id + stride]
        S.syncthreads()
        stride = stride >> 0x1

    if thread_id == 0:
        result[0] = shared_buf[0]


@substrate.jit
def kernel_shm_subview_view_offsets(result: S.Tensor((2,), S.u32)):
    shared_words = S.make_shared((16,), S.u32)
    left_words = S.subview(shared_words, (0,), (8,), (1,))
    right_words = S.subview(shared_words, (8,), (8,), (1,))
    layout = S.make_layout((2, 2), (2, 1))
    left = S.view(left_words, S.u32, layout)
    right = S.view(right_words, S.u32, layout)

    tid = S.thread_id(0)
    if tid == 0:
        left[0, 0] = S.convert(11, S.u32)
        right[0, 0] = S.convert(22, S.u32)

    S.syncthreads()

    if tid == 0:
        result[0] = left[0, 0]
        result[1] = right[0, 0]


@substrate.jit
def kernel_shm_subview_view_mixed_types(result: S.Tensor((4,), S.i32)):
    shared_words = S.make_shared((32,), S.u32)
    stats_words = S.subview(shared_words, (0,), (8,), (1,))
    q_words = S.subview(shared_words, (8,), (8,), (1,))
    kv_words = S.subview(shared_words, (16,), (8,), (1,))
    score_words = S.subview(shared_words, (24,), (8,), (1,))
    layout_f32 = S.make_layout((2, 4), (4, 1))
    layout_bf16 = S.make_layout((2, 4), (4, 1))
    layout_u32 = S.make_layout((2, 2), (2, 1))
    stats = S.view(stats_words, S.f32, layout_f32)
    q = S.view(q_words, S.bf16, layout_bf16)
    kv = S.view(kv_words, S.bf16, layout_bf16)
    score = S.view(score_words, S.f32, layout_f32)
    q_u32 = S.view(q_words, S.u32, layout_u32)
    kv_u32 = S.view(kv_words, S.u32, layout_u32)

    tid = S.thread_id(0)
    if tid == 0:
        stats[0, 0] = S.convert(3.0, S.f32)
        score[0, 0] = S.convert(4.0, S.f32)
        q[0, 0] = S.convert(1.0, S.bf16)
        q[0, 1] = S.convert(2.0, S.bf16)
        kv[0, 0] = S.convert(3.0, S.bf16)
        kv[0, 1] = S.convert(4.0, S.bf16)

    S.syncthreads()

    if tid == 0:
        result[0] = S.convert(stats[0, 0], S.i32)
        result[1] = q_u32[0, 0]
        result[2] = kv_u32[0, 0]
        result[3] = S.convert(score[0, 0], S.i32)


class TestSharedMemoryOps(unittest.TestCase):
    def test_basic_shared_memory(self):
        """Test basic shared memory read/write functionality"""
        input_data = torch.arange(32, dtype=torch.int32, device="cuda")
        output_data = torch.zeros(32, dtype=torch.int32, device="cuda")

        expected = torch.cat([input_data[1:], input_data[0:1]])

        kernel_shm_basic[lambda: ((1, 1, 1), (32, 1, 1))](input_data, output_data)

        actual = output_data.cpu()
        expected = expected.cpu()

        self.assertTrue(
            torch.equal(actual, expected),
            f"Expected: {expected.tolist()}, Actual: {actual.tolist()}",
        )

    def test_2d_shared_memory(self):
        """Test 2D shared memory with matrix transpose"""
        input_matrix = torch.arange(256, dtype=torch.float32, device="cuda").reshape(16, 16)
        output_matrix = torch.zeros((16, 16), dtype=torch.float32, device="cuda")

        expected = input_matrix.t()  # Transpose

        kernel_shm_2d[lambda: ((1, 1, 1), (16, 16, 1))](input_matrix, output_matrix)

        actual = output_matrix.cpu()
        expected = expected.cpu()

        self.assertTrue(
            torch.allclose(actual, expected),
            f"Max difference: {(actual - expected).abs().max()}",
        )

    def test_shm_reduction(self):
        """Test shared memory reduction operation"""
        input_data = torch.ones(32, dtype=torch.float32, device="cuda")
        result = torch.zeros(2, dtype=torch.float32, device="cuda")

        expected = torch.sum(input_data)

        kernel_shm_reduction[lambda: ((1, 1, 1), (32, 1, 1))](input_data, result)

        actual = result[0].cpu().item()
        expected = expected.cpu().item()

        self.assertAlmostEqual(actual, expected, places=5, msg=f"Expected: {expected}, Got: {actual}")

    def test_shm_subview_view_offsets(self):
        """Test that typed views preserve non-zero shared subview offsets."""
        result = torch.zeros(2, dtype=torch.int32, device="cuda")

        kernel_shm_subview_view_offsets[lambda: ((1, 1, 1), (32, 1, 1))](result)

        actual = result.cpu()
        expected = torch.tensor([11, 22], dtype=torch.int32)

def probe(
    A: S.Tensor((32,16), S.bf16),
    B: S.Tensor((16,32), S.bf16),
    O: S.Tensor((64,16), S.f32),

+        shared_a[a_row, a_col + i] = a_vals[i]
+
+    b_linear = tid * 8
+    b_row = b_linear // BLOCK_N
+    b_col = b_linear % BLOCK_N
+    b_offset = (b_row * N + block_col + b_col) * BF16_BYTES
+    b_pack = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(b_rsrc, zero, S.convert(b_offset, S.i32), 0)
+    b_vals = S.view(b_pack, S.Tensor((8,), S.bf16))
+    for i in S.range(8):
+        shared_b[b_row, b_col + i] = b_vals[i]
+
+    S.syncthreads()
+
+    acc = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+    wave_a_row = warp_row * 32 + (lane // 2)
+    wave_b_col = warp_col * 32 + ((lane % 4) * 8)
+
+    a_words0 = S.full((4,), 0, S.u32)
+    b_words0 = S.full((4,), 0, S.u32)
+    a_words1 = S.full((4,), 0, S.u32)
+    b_words1 = S.full((4,), 0, S.u32)
+
+    for i in S.range(4):
+        a_words0[i] = S.bitcast(shared_a[wave_a_row, (lane % 2) * 8 + i * 2], S.u32)
+        b_words0[i] = S.bitcast(shared_b[lane // 4, wave_b_col + i * 2], S.u32)
+        a_words1[i] = S.bitcast(shared_a[wave_a_row, 16 + (lane % 2) * 8 + i * 2], S.u32)
+        b_words1[i] = S.bitcast(shared_b[8 + lane // 4, wave_b_col + i * 2], S.u32)
 
+    a_frag0 = S.view(a_words0, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+    b_frag0 = S.view(b_words0, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+    a_frag1 = S.view(a_words1, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+    b_frag1 = S.view(b_words1, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
 
+    acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag0[0], b_frag0[0], acc)
+    acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag0[1], b_frag0[1], acc)
+    acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag1[0], b_frag1[0], acc)
+    acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag1[1], b_frag1[1], acc)
+
+    row_base0 = block_row + warp_row * 32 + (lane % 16)
+    row_base1 = row_base0 + 16
+    col_base = block_col + warp_col * 32 + (lane // 16) * 8
+
+    for i in S.range(4):
+        c0 = S.convert(acc[i], S.bf16)
+        c1 = S.convert(acc[4 + i], S.bf16)
+        c2 = S.convert(acc[8 + i], S.bf16)
+        c3 = S.convert(acc[12 + i], S.bf16)
+        C[row_base0, col_base + i] = c0
+        C[row_base1, col_base + i] = c1
+        C[row_base0, col_base + 4 + i] = c2
+        C[row_base1, col_base + 4 + i] = c3
+
+
+@substrate.jit
+def _probe_wave_accum(
+    A: S.Tensor((32, 16), S.bf16),
+    B: S.Tensor((16, 32), S.bf16),
+    O: S.Tensor((64, 16), S.f32),
+    a_range_bytes: S.i32,
+    b_range_bytes: S.i32,
+):
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    lane = tid
+    shared_a = S.make_shared((32, 16), S.bf16)
+    shared_b = S.make_shared((16, 32), S.bf16)
+    zero = S.convert(0, S.i32)
+
+    a_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(A, a_range_bytes)
+    b_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(B, b_range_bytes)
+
+    a_offset = tid * 16
+    b_offset = tid * 16
+    a_pack = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(a_rsrc, zero, S.convert(a_offset, S.i32), 0)
+    b_pack = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(b_rsrc, zero, S.convert(b_offset, S.i32), 0)
+    a_vals = S.view(a_pack, S.Tensor((8,), S.bf16))
+    b_vals = S.view(b_pack, S.Tensor((8,), S.bf16))
+
+    a_row = tid // 2
+    a_col = (tid % 2) * 8
+    b_row = tid // 4
+    b_col = (tid % 4) * 8
+    for i in S.range(8):
+        shared_a[a_row, a_col + i] = a_vals[i]
+        shared_b[b_row, b_col + i] = b_vals[i]
+    S.syncthreads()
+
+    a_words = S.full((4,), 0, S.u32)
+    b_words = S.full((4,), 0, S.u32)
+    for i in S.range(4):
+        a_words[i] = S.bitcast(shared_a[lane // 2, (lane % 2) * 8 + i * 2], S.u32)
+        b_words[i] = S.bitcast(shared_b[lane // 4, (lane % 4) * 8 + i * 2], S.u32)
+
+    a_frag = S.view(a_words, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+    b_frag = S.view(b_words, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+    acc = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+    acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[0], b_frag[0], acc)
+    acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[1], b_frag[1], acc)
+    O[lane] = acc
+
+
 class ModelNew(nn.Module):
     def __init__(self):
         super().__init__()
+        self._shape = (M, K, N)
+        self._launch = None
+        self._cached_ptrs = None
 
+    def _get_launch(self, A, B):
+        a_ptr = A.untyped_storage().data_ptr()
+        b_ptr = B.untyped_storage().data_ptr()
+        ptrs = (a_ptr, b_ptr)
+        if self._launch is None or self._cached_ptrs != ptrs:
+            self._cached_ptrs = ptrs
+            self._launch = gemm_kernel_mfma[lambda: ((N // BLOCK_N, M // BLOCK_M, 1), (THREADS_PER_BLOCK, 1, 1))]
+        return self._launch
+
     def forward(self, A, B):
-        if tuple(A.shape) != (32768, 32) or tuple(B.shape) != (32, 32768):
-            return torch.matmul(A, B)
         A = A.contiguous()
         B = B.contiguous()
-        C = torch.empty((32768, 32768), device=A.device, dtype=A.dtype)
-        gemm_kernel[lambda: ((1, 1, 1), (1, 1, 1))](A, B, C)
+        C = torch.empty((M, N), device=A.device, dtype=A.dtype)
+        launch = self._get_launch(A, B)
+        launch(
+            A,
+            B,
+            C,
+            A.numel() * A.element_size(),
+            B.numel() * B.element_size(),
+            C.numel() * C.element_size(),
+        )
         return C

+        C[row_base0, col_base + i] = c0
+        C[row_base1, col_base + i] = c1
+        C[row_base0, col_base + 4 + i] = c2
+        C[row_base1, col_base + 4 + i] = c3

+@substrate.jit
+def _probe_wave_accum(
+    A: S.Tensor((32, 16), S.bf16),
+    B: S.Tensor((16, 32), S.bf16),
+    O: S.Tensor((64, 16), S.f32),
+    a_range_bytes: S.i32,
+    b_range_bytes: S.i32,
+):
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    lane = tid
+    shared_a = S.make_shared((32, 16), S.bf16)
+    shared_b = S.make_shared((16, 32), S.bf16)
+    zero = S.convert(0, S.i32)
+
+    a_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(A, a_range_bytes)
+    b_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(B, b_range_bytes)
+
+    a_offset = tid * 16
+    b_offset = tid * 16
+    a_pack = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(a_rsrc, zero, S.convert(a_offset, S.i32), 0)
+    b_pack = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(b_rsrc, zero, S.convert(b_offset, S.i32), 0)
+    a_vals = S.view(a_pack, S.Tensor((8,), S.bf16))
+    b_vals = S.view(b_pack, S.Tensor((8,), S.bf16))
+
+    a_row = tid // 2
+    a_col = (tid % 2) * 8
+    b_row = tid // 4
+    b_col = (tid % 4) * 8
+    for i in S.range(8):
+        shared_a[a_row, a_col + i] = a_vals[i]
+        shared_b[b_row, b_col + i] = b_vals[i]
+    S.syncthreads()
+
+    a_words = S.full((4,), 0, S.u32)
+    b_words = S.full((4,), 0, S.u32)
+    for i in S.range(4):
+        a_words[i] = S.bitcast(shared_a[lane // 2, (lane % 2) * 8 + i * 2], S.u32)
+        b_words[i] = S.bitcast(shared_b[lane // 4, (lane % 4) * 8 + i * 2], S.u32)
+
+    a_frag = S.view(a_words, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+    b_frag = S.view(b_words, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+    acc = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+    acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[0], b_frag[0], acc)
+    acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[1], b_frag[1], acc)
+    O[lane] = acc

codex
The first compile failure is specific and useful: scalar `bf16 -> u32` bitcasts are invalid here. I’m replacing those scalar pack loops with typed `subview`+`view` loads from LDS, which is also closer to the intended 16-byte fragment handling.
apply patch

+    b_pack = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(b_rsrc, zero, S.convert(b_offset, S.i32), 0)
+    b_vals = S.view(b_pack, S.Tensor((8,), S.bf16))
+    for i in S.range(8):
+        shared_b[b_row, b_col + i] = b_vals[i]
+
+    S.syncthreads()
+
+    acc = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+    wave_a_row = warp_row * 32 + (lane // 2)
+    wave_b_col = warp_col * 32 + ((lane % 4) * 8)
+
+    a_frag0 = S.view(
+        S.subview(shared_a, (wave_a_row, (lane % 2) * 8), (1, 8), (1, 1)),
+        S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16),
+    )
+    b_frag0 = S.view(
+        S.subview(shared_b, (lane // 4, wave_b_col), (1, 8), (1, 1)),
+        S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16),
+    )
+    a_frag1 = S.view(
+        S.subview(shared_a, (wave_a_row, 16 + (lane % 2) * 8), (1, 8), (1, 1)),
+        S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16),
+    )
+    b_frag1 = S.view(
+        S.subview(shared_b, (8 + lane // 4, wave_b_col), (1, 8), (1, 1)),
+        S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16),
+    )
+
+    acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag0[0], b_frag0[0], acc)
+    acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag0[1], b_frag0[1], acc)
+    acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag1[0], b_frag1[0], acc)
+    acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag1[1], b_frag1[1], acc)
+
+    row_base0 = block_row + warp_row * 32 + (lane % 16)
+    row_base1 = row_base0 + 16
+    col_base = block_col + warp_col * 32 + (lane // 16) * 8
+
+    for i in S.range(4):
+        c0 = S.convert(acc[i], S.bf16)
+        c1 = S.convert(acc[4 + i], S.bf16)
+        c2 = S.convert(acc[8 + i], S.bf16)
+        c3 = S.convert(acc[12 + i], S.bf16)
+        C[row_base0, col_base + i] = c0
+        C[row_base1, col_base + i] = c1
+        C[row_base0, col_base + 4 + i] = c2
+        C[row_base1, col_base + 4 + i] = c3
+
+
+@substrate.jit
+def _probe_wave_accum(
+    A: S.Tensor((32, 16), S.bf16),
+    B: S.Tensor((16, 32), S.bf16),
+    O: S.Tensor((64, 16), S.f32),
+    a_range_bytes: S.i32,
+    b_range_bytes: S.i32,
 ):
-    for i in S.range(M):
-        for j in S.range(N):
-            acc = S.convert(0.0, S.f32)
-            for kk in S.range(K):
-                acc += S.convert(A[i, kk], S.f32) * S.convert(B[kk, j], S.f32)
-            C[i, j] = S.convert(acc, S.bf16)
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    lane = tid
+    shared_a = S.make_shared((32, 16), S.bf16)
+    shared_b = S.make_shared((16, 32), S.bf16)
+    zero = S.convert(0, S.i32)
+
+    a_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(A, a_range_bytes)
+    b_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(B, b_range_bytes)
+
+    a_offset = tid * 16
+    b_offset = tid * 16
+    a_pack = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(a_rsrc, zero, S.convert(a_offset, S.i32), 0)
+    b_pack = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(b_rsrc, zero, S.convert(b_offset, S.i32), 0)
+    a_vals = S.view(a_pack, S.Tensor((8,), S.bf16))
+    b_vals = S.view(b_pack, S.Tensor((8,), S.bf16))
+
+    a_row = tid // 2
+    a_col = (tid % 2) * 8
+    b_row = tid // 4
+    b_col = (tid % 4) * 8
+    for i in S.range(8):
+        shared_a[a_row, a_col + i] = a_vals[i]
+        shared_b[b_row, b_col + i] = b_vals[i]
+    S.syncthreads()
+
+    a_frag = S.view(
+        S.subview(shared_a, (lane // 2, (lane % 2) * 8), (1, 8), (1, 1)),
+        S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16),
+    )
+    b_frag = S.view(
+        S.subview(shared_b, (lane // 4, (lane % 4) * 8), (1, 8), (1, 1)),
+        S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16),
+    )
+    acc = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+    acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[0], b_frag[0], acc)
+    acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[1], b_frag[1], acc)
+    O[lane] = acc
 
 
 class ModelNew(nn.Module):
     def __init__(self):
         super().__init__()
+        self._shape = (M, K, N)
+        self._launch = None
+        self._cached_ptrs = None
+
+    def _get_launch(self, A, B):
+        a_ptr = A.untyped_storage().data_ptr()
+        b_ptr = B.untyped_storage().data_ptr()
+        ptrs = (a_ptr, b_ptr)
+        if self._launch is None or self._cached_ptrs != ptrs:
+            self._cached_ptrs = ptrs
+            self._launch = gemm_kernel_mfma[lambda: ((N // BLOCK_N, M // BLOCK_M, 1), (THREADS_PER_BLOCK, 1, 1))]
+        return self._launch
 
     def forward(self, A, B):
-        if tuple(A.shape) != (32768, 32) or tuple(B.shape) != (32, 32768):
-            return torch.matmul(A, B)
         A = A.contiguous()
         B = B.contiguous()
-        C = torch.empty((32768, 32768), device=A.device, dtype=A.dtype)
-        gemm_kernel[lambda: ((1, 1, 1), (1, 1, 1))](A, B, C)
+        C = torch.empty((M, N), device=A.device, dtype=A.dtype)
+        launch = self._get_launch(A, B)
+        launch(
+            A,
+            B,
+            C,
+            A.numel() * A.element_size(),
+            B.numel() * B.element_size(),
+            C.numel() * C.element_size(),
+        )
         return C

codex
The workgroup `subview` path is what the backend is rejecting. I’m switching LDS storage to packed `u32` words and moving each 16-byte fragment into private `u32[4]` before the `view`, which should preserve the requested fragment semantics and avoid the lowering issue.

+        shared_a[a_row, a_col + i] = a_vals[i]
+        shared_b[b_row, b_col + i] = b_vals[i]

+        S.subview(shared_a, (lane // 2, (lane % 2) * 8), (1, 8), (1, 1)),
+        S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16),

+        S.subview(shared_b, (lane // 4, (lane % 4) * 8), (1, 8), (1, 1)),

+    acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[0], b_frag[0], acc)
+    acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[1], b_frag[1], acc)
+    O[lane] = acc

import torch
import torch.nn as nn

import substrate
import substrate.language as S


M = 32768
K = 32
N = 32768

BLOCK_M = 64
BLOCK_N = 64
WAVE_SIZE = 64
WAVES_PER_BLOCK = 4
THREADS_PER_BLOCK = WAVE_SIZE * WAVES_PER_BLOCK
BF16_BYTES = 2


@substrate.jit
def gemm_kernel_mfma(
    A: S.Tensor((32768, 32), S.bf16),
    B: S.Tensor((32, 32768), S.bf16),
    C: S.Tensor((32768, 32768), S.bf16),
    a_range_bytes: S.i32,
    b_range_bytes: S.i32,
    c_range_bytes: S.i32,
):
    tid = S.thread_id(0)
    lane = tid % WAVE_SIZE
    warp = tid // WAVE_SIZE
    warp_row = warp // 2
    warp_col = warp % 2

    block_row = S.block_id(1) * BLOCK_M
    block_col = S.block_id(0) * BLOCK_N

    shared_a = S.make_shared((BLOCK_M, K), S.bf16)
    shared_b = S.make_shared((K, BLOCK_N), S.bf16)

    a_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(A, a_range_bytes)
    b_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(B, b_range_bytes)
    c_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(C, c_range_bytes)

    zero = S.convert(0, S.i32)

    a_linear = tid * 8
    a_row = a_linear // K
    a_col = a_linear % K
    a_offset = ((block_row + a_row) * K + a_col) * BF16_BYTES
    a_pack = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(a_rsrc, zero, S.convert(a_offset, S.i32), 0)
    a_vals = S.view(a_pack, S.Tensor((8,), S.bf16))
    for i in S.range(8):
        shared_a[a_row, a_col + i] = a_vals[i]

    b_linear = tid * 8
    b_row = b_linear // BLOCK_N
    b_col = b_linear % BLOCK_N
    b_offset = (b_row * N + block_col + b_col) * BF16_BYTES
    b_pack = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(b_rsrc, zero, S.convert(b_offset, S.i32), 0)
    b_vals = S.view(b_pack, S.Tensor((8,), S.bf16))
    for i in S.range(8):
        shared_b[b_row, b_col + i] = b_vals[i]

    S.syncthreads()

    acc = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
    wave_a_row = warp_row * 32 + (lane // 2)
    wave_b_col = warp_col * 32 + ((lane % 4) * 8)

    a_frag0 = S.view(
        S.subview(shared_a, (wave_a_row, (lane % 2) * 8), (1, 8), (1, 1)),
        S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16),
    )
    b_frag0 = S.view(
        S.subview(shared_b, (lane // 4, wave_b_col), (1, 8), (1, 1)),
        S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16),
    )
    a_frag1 = S.view(
        S.subview(shared_a, (wave_a_row, 16 + (lane % 2) * 8), (1, 8), (1, 1)),
        S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16),
    )
    b_frag1 = S.view(
        S.subview(shared_b, (8 + lane // 4, wave_b_col), (1, 8), (1, 1)),
        S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16),
    )

    acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag0[0], b_frag0[0], acc)
    acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag0[1], b_frag0[1], acc)
    acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag1[0], b_frag1[0], acc)
    acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag1[1], b_frag1[1], acc)

    row_base0 = block_row + warp_row * 32 + (lane % 16)
    row_base1 = row_base0 + 16
    col_base = block_col + warp_col * 32 + (lane // 16) * 8

    for i in S.range(4):
        c0 = S.convert(acc[i], S.bf16)
        c1 = S.convert(acc[4 + i], S.bf16)
        c2 = S.convert(acc[8 + i], S.bf16)
        c3 = S.convert(acc[12 + i], S.bf16)
        C[row_base0, col_base + i] = c0
        C[row_base1, col_base + i] = c1
        C[row_base0, col_base + 4 + i] = c2
        C[row_base1, col_base + 4 + i] = c3


@substrate.jit
def _probe_wave_accum(
    A: S.Tensor((32, 16), S.bf16),
    B: S.Tensor((16, 32), S.bf16),
    O: S.Tensor((64, 16), S.f32),
    a_range_bytes: S.i32,
    b_range_bytes: S.i32,
):
    tid = S.thread_id(0)
    lane = tid
    shared_a = S.make_shared((32, 16), S.bf16)
    shared_b = S.make_shared((16, 32), S.bf16)
    zero = S.convert(0, S.i32)

    a_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(A, a_range_bytes)
    b_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(B, b_range_bytes)

    a_offset = tid * 16
    b_offset = tid * 16
    a_pack = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(a_rsrc, zero, S.convert(a_offset, S.i32), 0)
    b_pack = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(b_rsrc, zero, S.convert(b_offset, S.i32), 0)
    a_vals = S.view(a_pack, S.Tensor((8,), S.bf16))
    b_vals = S.view(b_pack, S.Tensor((8,), S.bf16))

    a_row = tid // 2
    a_col = (tid % 2) * 8
    b_row = tid // 4
    b_col = (tid % 4) * 8
    for i in S.range(8):
        shared_a[a_row, a_col + i] = a_vals[i]
        shared_b[b_row, b_col + i] = b_vals[i]
    S.syncthreads()

    a_frag = S.view(
        S.subview(shared_a, (lane // 2, (lane % 2) * 8), (1, 8), (1, 1)),
        S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16),
    )
    b_frag = S.view(
        S.subview(shared_b, (lane // 4, (lane % 4) * 8), (1, 8), (1, 1)),
        S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16),
    )
    acc = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
    acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[0], b_frag[0], acc)
    acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[1], b_frag[1], acc)
    O[lane] = acc


class ModelNew(nn.Module):
    def __init__(self):
        super().__init__()
        self._shape = (M, K, N)
        self._launch = None
        self._cached_ptrs = None

    def _get_launch(self, A, B):
        a_ptr = A.untyped_storage().data_ptr()
        b_ptr = B.untyped_storage().data_ptr()
        ptrs = (a_ptr, b_ptr)
        if self._launch is None or self._cached_ptrs != ptrs:
            self._cached_ptrs = ptrs
            self._launch = gemm_kernel_mfma[lambda: ((N // BLOCK_N, M // BLOCK_M, 1), (THREADS_PER_BLOCK, 1, 1))]
        return self._launch

    def forward(self, A, B):
        A = A.contiguous()
        B = B.contiguous()
        C = torch.empty((M, N), device=A.device, dtype=A.dtype)
        launch = self._get_launch(A, B)
        launch(
            A,
            B,
            C,
            A.numel() * A.element_size(),
            B.numel() * B.element_size(),
            C.numel() * C.element_size(),
        )
        return C

+    wave_b_word_col = warp_col * 16 + ((lane % 4) * 4)
+    a_words0 = S.full((4,), 0, S.u32)
+    b_words0 = S.full((4,), 0, S.u32)
+    a_words1 = S.full((4,), 0, S.u32)
+    b_words1 = S.full((4,), 0, S.u32)
+    for i in S.range(4):
+        a_words0[i] = shared_a[wave_a_row, (lane % 2) * 4 + i]
+        b_words0[i] = shared_b[lane // 4, wave_b_word_col + i]
+        a_words1[i] = shared_a[wave_a_row, 8 + (lane % 2) * 4 + i]
+        b_words1[i] = shared_b[8 + lane // 4, wave_b_word_col + i]
+
+    a_frag0 = S.view(a_words0, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+    b_frag0 = S.view(b_words0, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+    a_frag1 = S.view(a_words1, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+    b_frag1 = S.view(b_words1, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+
+    acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag0[0], b_frag0[0], acc)
+    acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag0[1], b_frag0[1], acc)
+    acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag1[0], b_frag1[0], acc)
+    acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag1[1], b_frag1[1], acc)
+
+    row_base0 = block_row + warp_row * 32 + (lane % 16)
+    row_base1 = row_base0 + 16
+    col_base = block_col + warp_col * 32 + (lane // 16) * 8
+
+    for i in S.range(4):
+        c0 = S.convert(acc[i], S.bf16)
+        c1 = S.convert(acc[4 + i], S.bf16)
+        c2 = S.convert(acc[8 + i], S.bf16)
+        c3 = S.convert(acc[12 + i], S.bf16)
+        C[row_base0, col_base + i] = c0
+        C[row_base1, col_base + i] = c1
+        C[row_base0, col_base + 4 + i] = c2
+        C[row_base1, col_base + 4 + i] = c3
+
+
+@substrate.jit
+def _probe_wave_accum(
+    A: S.Tensor((32, 16), S.bf16),
+    B: S.Tensor((16, 32), S.bf16),
+    O: S.Tensor((64, 16), S.f32),
+    a_range_bytes: S.i32,
+    b_range_bytes: S.i32,

-    for i in S.range(M):

-                acc += S.convert(A[i, kk], S.f32) * S.convert(B[kk, j], S.f32)
-            C[i, j] = S.convert(acc, S.bf16)
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    lane = tid
+    shared_a = S.make_shared((32, 8), S.u32)
+    shared_b = S.make_shared((16, 16), S.u32)
+    zero = S.convert(0, S.i32)
+
+    a_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(A, a_range_bytes)
+    b_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(B, b_range_bytes)
 
+    a_offset = tid * 16
+    b_offset = tid * 16
+    a_pack = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(a_rsrc, zero, S.convert(a_offset, S.i32), 0)
+    b_pack = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(b_rsrc, zero, S.convert(b_offset, S.i32), 0)
+    a_vals = S.view(a_pack, S.Tensor((4,), S.u32))
+    b_vals = S.view(b_pack, S.Tensor((4,), S.u32))
 
+    a_row = tid // 2
+    a_col = (tid % 2) * 4
+    b_row = tid // 4
+    b_col = (tid % 4) * 4
+    for i in S.range(4):
+        shared_a[a_row, a_col + i] = a_vals[i]
+        shared_b[b_row, b_col + i] = b_vals[i]
+    S.syncthreads()
+
+    a_words = S.full((4,), 0, S.u32)
+    b_words = S.full((4,), 0, S.u32)
+    for i in S.range(4):
+        a_words[i] = shared_a[lane // 2, (lane % 2) * 4 + i]
+        b_words[i] = shared_b[lane // 4, (lane % 4) * 4 + i]
+    a_frag = S.view(a_words, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+    b_frag = S.view(b_words, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+    acc = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+    acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[0], b_frag[0], acc)
+    acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[1], b_frag[1], acc)
+    O[lane] = acc
+

 class ModelNew(nn.Module):
     def __init__(self):
         super().__init__()
+        self._shape = (M, K, N)
+        self._launch = None
+        self._cached_ptrs = None
 
+    def _get_launch(self, A, B):
+        a_ptr = A.untyped_storage().data_ptr()
+        b_ptr = B.untyped_storage().data_ptr()
+        ptrs = (a_ptr, b_ptr)
+        if self._launch is None or self._cached_ptrs != ptrs:
+            self._cached_ptrs = ptrs
+            self._launch = gemm_kernel_mfma[lambda: ((N // BLOCK_N, M // BLOCK_M, 1), (THREADS_PER_BLOCK, 1, 1))]
+        return self._launch
+
     def forward(self, A, B):
-        if tuple(A.shape) != (32768, 32) or tuple(B.shape) != (32, 32768):

         B = B.contiguous()
-        C = torch.empty((32768, 32768), device=A.device, dtype=A.dtype)

+        launch = self._get_launch(A, B)
+        launch(
+            A,
+            B,
+            C,
+            A.numel() * A.element_size(),
+            B.numel() * B.element_size(),
+            C.numel() * C.element_size(),
+        )
         return C

+    col_base = block_col + warp_col * 32 + (lane // 16) * 8
+
+    for i in S.range(4):
+        c0 = S.convert(acc[i], S.bf16)
+        c1 = S.convert(acc[4 + i], S.bf16)
+        c2 = S.convert(acc[8 + i], S.bf16)
+        c3 = S.convert(acc[12 + i], S.bf16)
+        C[row_base0, col_base + i] = c0
+        C[row_base1, col_base + i] = c1
+        C[row_base0, col_base + 4 + i] = c2
+        C[row_base1, col_base + 4 + i] = c3
+
+
+@substrate.jit
+def _probe_wave_accum(
+    A: S.Tensor((32, 16), S.bf16),
+    B: S.Tensor((16, 32), S.bf16),
+    O: S.Tensor((64, 16), S.f32),
+    a_range_bytes: S.i32,
+    b_range_bytes: S.i32,
 ):
-    for i in S.range(M):
-        for j in S.range(N):
-            acc = S.convert(0.0, S.f32)
-            for kk in S.range(K):
-                acc += S.convert(A[i, kk], S.f32) * S.convert(B[kk, j], S.f32)
-            C[i, j] = S.convert(acc, S.bf16)
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    lane = tid
+    shared_a = S.make_shared((32, 8), S.u32)
+    shared_b = S.make_shared((16, 16), S.u32)
+    zero = S.convert(0, S.i32)
+
+    a_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(A, a_range_bytes)
+    b_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(B, b_range_bytes)
 
+    a_offset = tid * 16
+    b_offset = tid * 16
+    a_pack = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(a_rsrc, zero, S.convert(a_offset, S.i32), 0)
+    b_pack = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(b_rsrc, zero, S.convert(b_offset, S.i32), 0)
+    a_vals = S.view(a_pack, S.Tensor((4,), S.u32))
+    b_vals = S.view(b_pack, S.Tensor((4,), S.u32))
 
+    a_row = tid // 2
+    a_col = (tid % 2) * 4
+    b_row = tid // 4
+    b_col = (tid % 4) * 4
+    for i in S.range(4):
+        shared_a[a_row, a_col + i] = a_vals[i]
+        shared_b[b_row, b_col + i] = b_vals[i]
+    S.syncthreads()
+
+    a_words = S.full((4,), 0, S.u32)
+    b_words = S.full((4,), 0, S.u32)
+    for i in S.range(4):
+        a_words[i] = shared_a[lane // 2, (lane % 2) * 4 + i]
+        b_words[i] = shared_b[lane // 4, (lane % 4) * 4 + i]
+    a_frag = S.view(a_words, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+    b_frag = S.view(b_words, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+    acc = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+    acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[0], b_frag[0], acc)
+    acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[1], b_frag[1], acc)
+    O[lane] = acc
+
+
 class ModelNew(nn.Module):
     def __init__(self):
         super().__init__()
+        self._shape = (M, K, N)
+        self._launch = None
+        self._cached_ptrs = None
 
+    def _get_launch(self, A, B):
+        a_ptr = A.untyped_storage().data_ptr()
+        b_ptr = B.untyped_storage().data_ptr()
+        ptrs = (a_ptr, b_ptr)
+        if self._launch is None or self._cached_ptrs != ptrs:
+            self._cached_ptrs = ptrs
+            self._launch = gemm_kernel_mfma[lambda: ((N // BLOCK_N, M // BLOCK_M, 1), (THREADS_PER_BLOCK, 1, 1))]
+        return self._launch
+
     def forward(self, A, B):
-        if tuple(A.shape) != (32768, 32) or tuple(B.shape) != (32, 32768):
-            return torch.matmul(A, B)
         A = A.contiguous()
         B = B.contiguous()
-        C = torch.empty((32768, 32768), device=A.device, dtype=A.dtype)
-        gemm_kernel[lambda: ((1, 1, 1), (1, 1, 1))](A, B, C)

+        launch = self._get_launch(A, B)
+        launch(
+            A,
+            B,
+            C,
+            A.numel() * A.element_size(),
+            B.numel() * B.element_size(),
+            C.numel() * C.element_size(),
+        )
         return C

codex
I’m stripping the probe down to the smallest compiling MFMA path: raw global `x4` loads straight into the per-lane fragments. Once I have the accumulator mapping from that, I can decide how much of the original LDS staging to keep in the final kernel without blocking on backend limitations.

import importlib.util
import torch
path='/workspace/kernel_benchmark/kb_eval_pipeline/runs/kb1/p09/optimization_rounds_no_invariants/round1/output_model_new.py'
spec=importlib.util.spec_from_file_location('mod', path)
mod=importlib.util.module_from_spec(spec)
spec.loader.exec_module(mod)

def run(case):
    A=torch.zeros((32,16), device='cuda', dtype=torch.bfloat16)
    B=torch.zeros((16,32), device='cuda', dtype=torch.bfloat16)
    O=torch.zeros((64,16), device='cuda', dtype=torch.float32)
    if case==0:
        A[:,0]=torch.arange(1,33, device='cuda', dtype=torch.float32).to(torch.bfloat16)
        B[0,:]=1
    else:
        A[:,1]=1
        B[1,:]=torch.arange(1,33, device='cuda', dtype=torch.float32).to(torch.bfloat16)
    mod._probe_wave_accum[lambda: ((1,1,1),(64,1,1))](A,B,O,A.numel()*A.element_size(),B.numel()*B.element_size())
    return O.cpu()
R=run(0)
C=run(1)
for lane in [0,1,2,3,4,5,16,17,32,48]:
    print('lane', lane)
    print('row', R[lane].tolist())
    print('col', C[lane].tolist())
PY" in /workspace/kernel_benchmark

+    shared_a = S.make_shared((BLOCK_M, K // 2), S.u32)
+    shared_b = S.make_shared((K, BLOCK_N // 2), S.u32)
+
+    a_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(A, a_range_bytes)
+    b_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(B, b_range_bytes)
+    c_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(C, c_range_bytes)
+
+    zero = S.convert(0, S.i32)
+
+    a_linear = tid * 8
+    a_row = a_linear // K
+    a_col = a_linear % K
+    a_offset = ((block_row + a_row) * K + a_col) * BF16_BYTES
+    a_pack = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(a_rsrc, zero, S.convert(a_offset, S.i32), 0)
+    a_vals = S.view(a_pack, S.Tensor((4,), S.u32))
+    a_word_col = a_col // 2
+    for i in S.range(4):
+        shared_a[a_row, a_word_col + i] = a_vals[i]
 
+    b_linear = tid * 8
+    b_row = b_linear // BLOCK_N
+    b_col = b_linear % BLOCK_N
+    b_offset = (b_row * N + block_col + b_col) * BF16_BYTES
+    b_pack = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(b_rsrc, zero, S.convert(b_offset, S.i32), 0)
+    b_vals = S.view(b_pack, S.Tensor((4,), S.u32))
+    b_word_col = b_col // 2
+    for i in S.range(4):
+        shared_b[b_row, b_word_col + i] = b_vals[i]
+
+    S.syncthreads()
+
+    acc = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+    wave_a_row = warp_row * 32 + (lane // 2)
+    wave_b_word_col = warp_col * 16 + ((lane % 4) * 4)
+    a_words0 = S.full((4,), 0, S.u32)
+    b_words0 = S.full((4,), 0, S.u32)
+    a_words1 = S.full((4,), 0, S.u32)
+    b_words1 = S.full((4,), 0, S.u32)
+    for i in S.range(4):
+        a_words0[i] = shared_a[wave_a_row, (lane % 2) * 4 + i]
+        b_words0[i] = shared_b[lane // 4, wave_b_word_col + i]
+        a_words1[i] = shared_a[wave_a_row, 8 + (lane % 2) * 4 + i]
+        b_words1[i] = shared_b[8 + lane // 4, wave_b_word_col + i]
+
+    a_frag0 = S.view(a_words0, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+    b_frag0 = S.view(b_words0, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+    a_frag1 = S.view(a_words1, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+    b_frag1 = S.view(b_words1, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
 
+    acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag0[0], b_frag0[0], acc)
+    acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag0[1], b_frag0[1], acc)
+    acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag1[0], b_frag1[0], acc)
+    acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag1[1], b_frag1[1], acc)
+
+    row_base0 = block_row + warp_row * 32 + (lane % 16)
+    row_base1 = row_base0 + 16
+    col_base = block_col + warp_col * 32 + (lane // 16) * 8
+
+    for i in S.range(4):
+        c0 = S.convert(acc[i], S.bf16)
+        c1 = S.convert(acc[4 + i], S.bf16)
+        c2 = S.convert(acc[8 + i], S.bf16)
+        c3 = S.convert(acc[12 + i], S.bf16)
+        C[row_base0, col_base + i] = c0
+        C[row_base1, col_base + i] = c1
+        C[row_base0, col_base + 4 + i] = c2
+        C[row_base1, col_base + 4 + i] = c3
+
+
+@substrate.jit
+def _probe_wave_accum(
+    A: S.Tensor((32, 16), S.bf16),
+    B: S.Tensor((16, 32), S.bf16),
+    O: S.Tensor((64, 16), S.f32),
+    a_range_bytes: S.i32,
+    b_range_bytes: S.i32,

+    b_pack = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(b_rsrc, zero, S.convert(b_offset, S.i32), 0)
+    a_frag = S.view(a_pack, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))

+    acc = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+    acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[0], b_frag[0], acc)
+    acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[1], b_frag[1], acc)
+    O[lane] = acc

     def __init__(self):

codex
The backend is compiling MFMA itself; the remaining problem is the exact operand/writeback layout. At this point the minimal, concrete unblocker is to inspect the local Substrate AMD GEMM implementation the test file already points at and lift only the needed lane/LDS mapping into this standalone kernel.

+    a_word_col = a_col // 2
+    for i in S.range(4):
+        shared_a[a_row, a_word_col + i] = a_vals[i]
 
+    b_linear = tid * 8
+    b_row = b_linear // BLOCK_N
+    b_col = b_linear % BLOCK_N
+    b_offset = (b_row * N + block_col + b_col) * BF16_BYTES
+    b_pack = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(b_rsrc, zero, S.convert(b_offset, S.i32), 0)
+    b_vals = S.view(b_pack, S.Tensor((4,), S.u32))
+    b_word_col = b_col // 2
+    for i in S.range(4):
+        shared_b[b_row, b_word_col + i] = b_vals[i]
+
+    S.syncthreads()
+
+    acc = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+    wave_a_row = warp_row * 32 + (lane // 2)
+    wave_b_word_col = warp_col * 16 + ((lane % 4) * 4)
+    a_words0 = S.full((4,), 0, S.u32)
+    b_words0 = S.full((4,), 0, S.u32)
+    a_words1 = S.full((4,), 0, S.u32)
+    b_words1 = S.full((4,), 0, S.u32)
+    for i in S.range(4):
+        a_words0[i] = shared_a[wave_a_row, (lane % 2) * 4 + i]
+        b_words0[i] = shared_b[lane // 4, wave_b_word_col + i]
+        a_words1[i] = shared_a[wave_a_row, 8 + (lane % 2) * 4 + i]
+        b_words1[i] = shared_b[8 + lane // 4, wave_b_word_col + i]
+
+    a_frag0 = S.view(a_words0, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+    b_frag0 = S.view(b_words0, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+    a_frag1 = S.view(a_words1, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+    b_frag1 = S.view(b_words1, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
 
+    acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag0[0], b_frag0[0], acc)
+    acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag0[1], b_frag0[1], acc)
+    acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag1[0], b_frag1[0], acc)
+    acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag1[1], b_frag1[1], acc)
+
+    row_base0 = block_row + warp_row * 32 + (lane % 16)
+    row_base1 = row_base0 + 16
+    col_base = block_col + warp_col * 32 + (lane // 16) * 8
+
+    for i in S.range(4):
+        c0 = S.convert(acc[i], S.bf16)
+        c1 = S.convert(acc[4 + i], S.bf16)
+        c2 = S.convert(acc[8 + i], S.bf16)
+        c3 = S.convert(acc[12 + i], S.bf16)
+        C[row_base0, col_base + i] = c0
+        C[row_base1, col_base + i] = c1
+        C[row_base0, col_base + 4 + i] = c2
+        C[row_base1, col_base + 4 + i] = c3
+
+
+@substrate.jit
+def _probe_wave_accum(
+    A: S.Tensor((32, 16), S.bf16),
+    B: S.Tensor((16, 32), S.bf16),
+    O: S.Tensor((64, 16), S.f32),
+    a_range_bytes: S.i32,
+    b_range_bytes: S.i32,
+):
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    lane = tid
+    zero = S.convert(0, S.i32)
+
+    a_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(A, a_range_bytes)
+    b_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(B, b_range_bytes)
+
+    a_offset = tid * 16
+    b_offset = tid * 16
+    a_pack = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(a_rsrc, zero, S.convert(a_offset, S.i32), 0)
+    b_pack = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(b_rsrc, zero, S.convert(b_offset, S.i32), 0)
+    a_frag = S.view(a_pack, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+    b_frag = S.view(b_pack, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+    acc = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+    acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[0], b_frag[0], acc)
+    acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[1], b_frag[1], acc)
+    O[lane] = acc
+
+
 class ModelNew(nn.Module):
     def __init__(self):
         super().__init__()
+        self._shape = (M, K, N)
+        self._launch = None
+        self._cached_ptrs = None
+
+    def _get_launch(self, A, B):
+        a_ptr = A.untyped_storage().data_ptr()
+        b_ptr = B.untyped_storage().data_ptr()
+        ptrs = (a_ptr, b_ptr)
+        if self._launch is None or self._cached_ptrs != ptrs:
+            self._cached_ptrs = ptrs
+            self._launch = gemm_kernel_mfma[lambda: ((N // BLOCK_N, M // BLOCK_M, 1), (THREADS_PER_BLOCK, 1, 1))]
+        return self._launch
 
     def forward(self, A, B):
-        if tuple(A.shape) != (32768, 32) or tuple(B.shape) != (32, 32768):
-            return torch.matmul(A, B)
         A = A.contiguous()
         B = B.contiguous()
-        C = torch.empty((32768, 32768), device=A.device, dtype=A.dtype)
-        gemm_kernel[lambda: ((1, 1, 1), (1, 1, 1))](A, B, C)
+        C = torch.empty((M, N), device=A.device, dtype=A.dtype)
+        launch = self._get_launch(A, B)
+        launch(
+            A,
+            B,
+            C,
+            A.numel() * A.element_size(),
+            B.numel() * B.element_size(),
+            C.numel() * C.element_size(),
+        )
         return C

#!/usr/bin/env python3
import unittest

import torch

from substrate_kernels import amdgpu_gemm


class TestGEMM(unittest.TestCase):
    def setUp(self):
        """Set up test fixtures before each test method."""
        torch.manual_seed(0)
        self.rtol = 1e-2
        self.atol = 1e-3

    def _assert_matches_reference(self, actual, expected):
        self.assertTrue(
            torch.allclose(actual, expected, rtol=self.rtol, atol=self.atol),
            msg=f"GEMM results do not match.\nExpected:\n{expected}\nActual:\n{actual}\n"
            f"Max absolute difference: {torch.max(torch.abs(actual - expected))}",
        )

    def test_gemm_1stage_row_major_and_transposed_b(self):
        for m, n, k in ((256, 256, 128), (512, 512, 256)):
            with self.subTest(m=m, n=n, k=k):
                A = torch.randn((m, k), dtype=torch.bfloat16, device="cuda")
                B = torch.randn((k, n), dtype=torch.bfloat16, device="cuda")
                B_t = B.t().contiguous()
                expected = (A @ B).to(dtype=torch.bfloat16, device="cpu")

                actual_row_major = amdgpu_gemm.gemm_1stage_pipeline_row_major(A, B).to("cpu")
                actual_transposed = amdgpu_gemm.gemm_1stage_pipeline_transposed_b(A, B_t).to("cpu")
                actual_alias = amdgpu_gemm.gemm_1stage_pipeline(A, B).to("cpu")

                self._assert_matches_reference(actual_row_major, expected)
                self._assert_matches_reference(actual_transposed, expected)
                self._assert_matches_reference(actual_alias, expected)

    def test_bmm_1stage_row_major_and_transposed_b(self):
        for batch, m, n, k in ((2, 256, 256, 128), (3, 512, 512, 256)):
            with self.subTest(batch=batch, m=m, n=n, k=k):
                A = torch.randn((batch, m, k), dtype=torch.bfloat16, device="cuda")
                B = torch.randn((batch, k, n), dtype=torch.bfloat16, device="cuda")
                B_t = B.transpose(1, 2).contiguous()
                expected = torch.bmm(A, B).to(dtype=torch.bfloat16, device="cpu")

                actual_row_major = amdgpu_gemm.gemm_1stage_pipeline_row_major(A, B).to("cpu")
                actual_transposed = amdgpu_gemm.gemm_1stage_pipeline_transposed_b(A, B_t).to("cpu")
                actual_alias = amdgpu_gemm.gemm_1stage_pipeline(A, B).to("cpu")

                self._assert_matches_reference(actual_row_major, expected)
                self._assert_matches_reference(actual_transposed, expected)
                self._assert_matches_reference(actual_alias, expected)

    def test_row_major_entrypoint_rejects_transposed_b_layout(self):
        m = 256
        n = 512
        k = 128
        A = torch.randn((m, k), dtype=torch.bfloat16, device="cuda")
        B = torch.randn((k, n), dtype=torch.bfloat16, device="cuda")

        with self.assertRaisesRegex(ValueError, r"standard row-major GEMM shape"):
            amdgpu_gemm.gemm_1stage_pipeline_row_major(A, B.t().contiguous())

    def test_transposed_b_entrypoint_rejects_row_major_b_layout(self):
        m = 256
        n = 512
        k = 128
        A = torch.randn((m, k), dtype=torch.bfloat16, device="cuda")
        B = torch.randn((k, n), dtype=torch.bfloat16, device="cuda")

        with self.assertRaisesRegex(ValueError, r"transposed B must have shape"):
            amdgpu_gemm.gemm_1stage_pipeline_transposed_b(A, B)

    def test_batched_row_major_entrypoint_rejects_transposed_b_layout(self):
        batch = 2
        m = 256
        n = 512
        k = 128
        A = torch.randn((batch, m, k), dtype=torch.bfloat16, device="cuda")
        B = torch.randn((batch, k, n), dtype=torch.bfloat16, device="cuda")

        with self.assertRaisesRegex(ValueError, r"batched row-major GEMM"):
            amdgpu_gemm.gemm_1stage_pipeline_row_major(A, B.transpose(1, 2).contiguous())

    def test_batched_transposed_b_entrypoint_rejects_row_major_b_layout(self):
        batch = 2
        m = 256
        n = 512
        k = 128
        A = torch.randn((batch, m, k), dtype=torch.bfloat16, device="cuda")
        B = torch.randn((batch, k, n), dtype=torch.bfloat16, device="cuda")

        with self.assertRaisesRegex(ValueError, r"batched transposed GEMM"):
            amdgpu_gemm.gemm_1stage_pipeline_transposed_b(A, B)


if __name__ == "__main__":
    unittest.main()

+    b_vals = S.view(b_pack, S.Tensor((4,), S.u32))
+    b_word_col = b_col // 2
+    for i in S.range(4):
+        shared_b[b_row, b_word_col + i] = b_vals[i]
+
+    S.syncthreads()
+
+    acc = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+    wave_a_row = warp_row * 32 + (lane // 2)
+    wave_b_word_col = warp_col * 16 + ((lane % 4) * 4)
+    a_words0 = S.full((4,), 0, S.u32)
+    b_words0 = S.full((4,), 0, S.u32)
+    a_words1 = S.full((4,), 0, S.u32)
+    b_words1 = S.full((4,), 0, S.u32)
+    for i in S.range(4):
+        a_words0[i] = shared_a[wave_a_row, (lane % 2) * 4 + i]
+        b_words0[i] = shared_b[lane // 4, wave_b_word_col + i]
+        a_words1[i] = shared_a[wave_a_row, 8 + (lane % 2) * 4 + i]
+        b_words1[i] = shared_b[8 + lane // 4, wave_b_word_col + i]
+
+    a_frag0 = S.view(a_words0, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+    b_frag0 = S.view(b_words0, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+    a_frag1 = S.view(a_words1, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+    b_frag1 = S.view(b_words1, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
 
+    acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag0[0], b_frag0[0], acc)
+    acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag0[1], b_frag0[1], acc)
+    acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag1[0], b_frag1[0], acc)
+    acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag1[1], b_frag1[1], acc)
+
+    row_base0 = block_row + warp_row * 32 + (lane % 16)
+    row_base1 = row_base0 + 16
+    col_base = block_col + warp_col * 32 + (lane // 16) * 8
+
+    for i in S.range(4):
+        c0 = S.convert(acc[i], S.bf16)
+        c1 = S.convert(acc[4 + i], S.bf16)
+        c2 = S.convert(acc[8 + i], S.bf16)
+        c3 = S.convert(acc[12 + i], S.bf16)
+        C[row_base0, col_base + i] = c0
+        C[row_base1, col_base + i] = c1
+        C[row_base0, col_base + 4 + i] = c2
+        C[row_base1, col_base + 4 + i] = c3
+

+@substrate.jit
+def _probe_wave_accum(
+    A: S.Tensor((32, 16), S.bf16),
+    B: S.Tensor((16, 32), S.bf16),
+    O: S.Tensor((64, 16), S.f32),

+    O[lane] = acc

     def __init__(self):

codex
I’ve got a workable path now: keep row-major `x4` global loads into LDS, then gather the exact per-lane MFMA fragments from LDS with a discovered mapping table. I’m adding a tiny fragment-space probe kernel so I can infer that mapping once and bake it into the final kernel.
apply patch

import importlib.util, torch, math
path='/workspace/kernel_benchmark/kb_eval_pipeline/runs/kb1/p09/optimization_rounds_no_invariants/round1/output_model_new.py'

def pack_bf16(mat):
    return mat.contiguous().view(torch.uint32)

# Unique values for B fragment positions
Bbf = torch.arange(1, 64*8+1, device='cuda', dtype=torch.float32).reshape(64,8).to(torch.bfloat16)
B = pack_bf16(Bbf)
O = torch.zeros((64,16), device='cuda', dtype=torch.float32)
row_sets = []
for p in range(64*8):
    Abf = torch.zeros((64,8), device='cuda', dtype=torch.bfloat16)
    Abf.view(-1)[p] = 1
    A = pack_bf16(Abf)
    mod._probe_frag_accum[lambda: ((1,1,1),(64,1,1))](A,B,O)
    vals = O.cpu().view(-1)
    nz = torch.nonzero(vals).view(-1).tolist()
    row_sets.append((p, nz, vals[nz].tolist()))
    if p % 64 == 0:
        print('p', p)
        print('nz count', len(nz), 'sample', nz[:8], vals[nz[:8]].tolist())
        break

/bin/bash -lc "python - <<'PY'
import importlib.util, torch, collections
path='/workspace/kernel_benchmark/kb_eval_pipeline/runs/kb1/p09/optimization_rounds_no_invariants/round1/output_model_new.py'
spec=importlib.util.spec_from_file_location('mod', path)
mod=importlib.util.module_from_spec(spec)
spec.loader.exec_module(mod)

kernel = mod._probe_frag_accum[lambda: ((1,1,1),(64,1,1))]

def pack_bf16(mat):
    return mat.contiguous().view(torch.uint32)

O = torch.zeros((64,16), device='cuda', dtype=torch.float32)
# A single hot, B unique
Bbf = torch.arange(1, 64*8+1, device='cuda', dtype=torch.float32).reshape(64,8).to(torch.bfloat16)
B = pack_bf16(Bbf)
A_sets = []
A_vals = []
for p in range(64*8):
    Abf = torch.zeros((64,8), device='cuda', dtype=torch.bfloat16)
    Abf.view(-1)[p] = 1
    A = pack_bf16(Abf)
    kernel(A,B,O)
    vals = O.cpu().view(-1)
    nz = torch.nonzero(vals).view(-1)
    A_sets.append(tuple(nz.tolist()))
    A_vals.append(tuple(int(round(v)) for v in vals[nz].tolist()))

# B single hot, A unique
Abf = torch.arange(1, 64*8+1, device='cuda', dtype=torch.float32).reshape(64,8).to(torch.bfloat16)
A = pack_bf16(Abf)
B_sets = []
B_vals = []
for p in range(64*8):
    Bbf = torch.zeros((64,8), device='cuda', dtype=torch.bfloat16)
    Bbf.view(-1)[p] = 1
    B = pack_bf16(Bbf)
    kernel(A,B,O)
    vals = O.cpu().view(-1)
    nz = torch.nonzero(vals).view(-1)
    B_sets.append(tuple(nz.tolist()))
    B_vals.append(tuple(int(round(v)) for v in vals[nz].tolist()))

row_groups = {}
for p,s in enumerate(A_sets): row_groups.setdefault(s, []).append(p)
col_groups = {}
for p,s in enumerate(B_sets): col_groups.setdefault(s, []).append(p)
print('row groups', len(row_groups), 'sizes', sorted({len(v) for v in row_groups.values()}))
print('col groups', len(col_groups), 'sizes', sorted({len(v) for v in col_groups.values()}))

# build k-components graph by A->B values edges
adjA=[set(v_i-1 for v_i in vals) for vals in A_vals]
adjB=[set() for _ in range(64*8)]
for a,bs in enumerate(adjA):
    for b in bs: adjB[b].add(a)
visitedA=set(); visitedB=set(); comps=[]
for a0 in range(64*8):
    if a0 in visitedA: continue
    qa=[a0]; As=set(); Bs=set()
    while qa:
        a=qa.pop()
        if a in visitedA: continue
        visitedA.add(a); As.add(a)
        for b in adjA[a]:
            if b not in visitedB:
                visitedB.add(b); Bs.add(b)
                for a2 in adjB[b]:
                    if a2 not in visitedA: qa.append(a2)
    comps.append((sorted(As), sorted(Bs)))
print('k comps', len(comps), 'A sizes', sorted({len(a) for a,b in comps}), 'B sizes', sorted({len(b) for a,b in comps}))

# label rows/cols/k
row_keys=list(row_groups.keys())
col_keys=list(col_groups.keys())
row_id={p:i for i,key in enumerate(row_keys) for p in row_groups[key]}
col_id={p:i for i,key in enumerate(col_keys) for p in col_groups[key]}
k_id={}
for i,(As,Bs) in enumerate(comps):
    for p in As: k_id=('A',p),i
    for p in Bs: k_id=('B',p),i

# print sample mappings for pattern discovery
print('A first 32:')
for p in range(32):
    kid=[i for i,(As,Bs) in enumerate(comps) if p in As][0]
    print(p, 'row', row_id[p], 'k', kid)
print('B first 32:')
for p in range(32):
    kid=[i for i,(As,Bs) in enumerate(comps) if p in Bs][0]
    print(p, 'col', col_id[p], 'k', kid)

# output mapping via row/col set intersections
row_sets=list(row_groups.keys())
col_sets=list(col_groups.keys())
out_map={}
for ri,rset in enumerate(row_sets):
    rs=set(rset)
    for ci,cset in enumerate(col_sets):
        inter=rs & set(cset)
        if len(inter)"'!=1:
            continue
        out_map[next(iter(inter))]=(ri,ci)
print('"'out mapped', len(out_map))
for p in range(32):
    print('O', p, out_map.get(p))

     def __init__(self):

+        self._shape = (M, K, N)

+        self._cached_ptrs = None

+    acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag1[1], b_frag1[1], acc)
+
+    row_base0 = block_row + warp_row * 32 + (lane % 16)
+    row_base1 = row_base0 + 16
+    col_base = block_col + warp_col * 32 + (lane // 16) * 8
+
+    for i in S.range(4):
+        c0 = S.convert(acc[i], S.bf16)
+        c1 = S.convert(acc[4 + i], S.bf16)
+        c2 = S.convert(acc[8 + i], S.bf16)
+        c3 = S.convert(acc[12 + i], S.bf16)
+        C[row_base0, col_base + i] = c0
+        C[row_base1, col_base + i] = c1
+        C[row_base0, col_base + 4 + i] = c2
+        C[row_base1, col_base + 4 + i] = c3
+
+
+@substrate.jit
+def _probe_wave_accum(
+    A: S.Tensor((32, 16), S.bf16),
+    B: S.Tensor((16, 32), S.bf16),
+    O: S.Tensor((64, 16), S.f32),
+    a_range_bytes: S.i32,
+    b_range_bytes: S.i32,
 ):
-    for i in S.range(M):
-        for j in S.range(N):
-            acc = S.convert(0.0, S.f32)
-            for kk in S.range(K):
-                acc += S.convert(A[i, kk], S.f32) * S.convert(B[kk, j], S.f32)
-            C[i, j] = S.convert(acc, S.bf16)
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    lane = tid
+    zero = S.convert(0, S.i32)
+
+    a_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(A, a_range_bytes)
+    b_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(B, b_range_bytes)
+
+    a_offset = tid * 16
+    b_offset = tid * 16
+    a_pack = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(a_rsrc, zero, S.convert(a_offset, S.i32), 0)
+    b_pack = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(b_rsrc, zero, S.convert(b_offset, S.i32), 0)
+    a_frag = S.view(a_pack, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+    b_frag = S.view(b_pack, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+    acc = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+    acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[0], b_frag[0], acc)
+    acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[1], b_frag[1], acc)
+    O[lane] = acc
 
 
+@substrate.jit
+def _probe_frag_accum(
+    A: S.Tensor((64, 4), S.u32),
+    B: S.Tensor((64, 4), S.u32),
+    O: S.Tensor((64, 16), S.f32),
+):
+    lane = S.thread_id(0)
+    a_frag = S.view(A[lane], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+    b_frag = S.view(B[lane], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+    acc = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+    acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[0], b_frag[0], acc)
+    acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[1], b_frag[1], acc)
+    O[lane] = acc
+
+
 class ModelNew(nn.Module):
     def __init__(self):
         super().__init__()
+        self._shape = (M, K, N)
+        self._launch = None
+        self._cached_ptrs = None
+
+    def _get_launch(self, A, B):
+        a_ptr = A.untyped_storage().data_ptr()
+        b_ptr = B.untyped_storage().data_ptr()
+        ptrs = (a_ptr, b_ptr)
+        if self._launch is None or self._cached_ptrs != ptrs:
+            self._cached_ptrs = ptrs
+            self._launch = gemm_kernel_mfma[lambda: ((N // BLOCK_N, M // BLOCK_M, 1), (THREADS_PER_BLOCK, 1, 1))]
+        return self._launch
 
     def forward(self, A, B):
-        if tuple(A.shape) != (32768, 32) or tuple(B.shape) != (32, 32768):
-            return torch.matmul(A, B)
         A = A.contiguous()
         B = B.contiguous()
-        C = torch.empty((32768, 32768), device=A.device, dtype=A.dtype)
-        gemm_kernel[lambda: ((1, 1, 1), (1, 1, 1))](A, B, C)

+        launch = self._get_launch(A, B)
+        launch(
+            A,
+            B,
+            C,
+            A.numel() * A.element_size(),
+            B.numel() * B.element_size(),
+            C.numel() * C.element_size(),
+        )
         return C

codex
I have the MFMA lane mapping now. The final kernel patch is straightforward: row-major `x4` loads into LDS, per-wave scalar gathers from LDS into private 8-element bf16 fragments, two natural MFMA steps per 16-K chunk, and the exact accumulator scatter discovered from the probe.
apply patch

+THREADS_PER_BLOCK = WAVE_SIZE * WAVES_PER_BLOCK

 @substrate.jit
-def gemm_kernel(
+def gemm_kernel_mfma(
     A: S.Tensor((32768, 32), S.bf16),
     B: S.Tensor((32, 32768), S.bf16),
     C: S.Tensor((32768, 32768), S.bf16),
+    a_range_bytes: S.i32,
+    b_range_bytes: S.i32,
+):
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    lane = tid % WAVE_SIZE
+    warp = tid // WAVE_SIZE
+    warp_row = warp // 2
+    warp_col = warp % 2
+
+    block_row = S.block_id(1) * BLOCK_M
+    block_col = S.block_id(0) * BLOCK_N
+
+    shared_a = S.make_shared((BLOCK_M, K), S.bf16)
+    shared_b = S.make_shared((K, BLOCK_N), S.bf16)
+
+    a_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(A, a_range_bytes)
+    b_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(B, b_range_bytes)
+
+    zero = S.convert(0, S.i32)
+
+    a_linear = tid * 8
+    a_row = a_linear // K
+    a_col = a_linear % K
+    a_offset = ((block_row + a_row) * K + a_col) * BF16_BYTES
+    a_pack = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(a_rsrc, zero, S.convert(a_offset, S.i32), 0)
+    a_vals = S.view(a_pack, S.Tensor((8,), S.bf16))
+    for i in S.range(8):
+        shared_a[a_row, a_col + i] = a_vals[i]
+
+    b_linear = tid * 8
+    b_row = b_linear // BLOCK_N
+    b_col = b_linear % BLOCK_N
+    b_offset = (b_row * N + block_col + b_col) * BF16_BYTES
+    b_pack = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(b_rsrc, zero, S.convert(b_offset, S.i32), 0)
+    b_vals = S.view(b_pack, S.Tensor((8,), S.bf16))
+    for i in S.range(8):
+        shared_b[b_row, b_col + i] = b_vals[i]
+
+    S.syncthreads()
+
+    acc = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+    wave_row = warp_row * 32
+    wave_col = warp_col * 32
+    lane_row = lane % 32
+    lane_col = lane % 32
+    lane_k8 = (lane // 32) * 8
+
+    for phase in S.range(2):
+        a_frag_words = S.full((8,), S.convert(0.0, S.bf16), S.bf16)
+        b_frag_words = S.full((8,), S.convert(0.0, S.bf16), S.bf16)
+        phase_k = phase * 16 + lane_k8
+        for i in S.range(8):
+            a_frag_words[i] = shared_a[wave_row + lane_row, phase_k + i]
+            b_frag_words[i] = shared_b[phase_k + i, wave_col + lane_col]
+
+        a_frag = S.view(a_frag_words, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+        b_frag = S.view(b_frag_words, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+        acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[0], b_frag[0], acc)
+        acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[1], b_frag[1], acc)
+
+    out_col = block_col + wave_col + lane_col
+    row_group = (lane // 32) * 4
+    for i in S.range(16):
+        out_row = block_row + wave_row + (i // 4) * 8 + row_group + (i % 4)
+        C[out_row, out_col] = S.convert(acc[i], S.bf16)
+

+@substrate.jit
+def _probe_wave_accum(
+    A: S.Tensor((32, 16), S.bf16),
+    B: S.Tensor((16, 32), S.bf16),
+    O: S.Tensor((64, 16), S.f32),

-                acc += S.convert(A[i, kk], S.f32) * S.convert(B[kk, j], S.f32)
-            C[i, j] = S.convert(acc, S.bf16)
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    lane = tid
+    zero = S.convert(0, S.i32)
 
+    a_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(A, a_range_bytes)
+    b_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(B, b_range_bytes)
+
+    a_offset = tid * 16
+    b_offset = tid * 16
+    a_pack = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(a_rsrc, zero, S.convert(a_offset, S.i32), 0)
+    b_pack = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(b_rsrc, zero, S.convert(b_offset, S.i32), 0)
+    a_frag = S.view(a_pack, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+    b_frag = S.view(b_pack, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+    acc = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+    acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[0], b_frag[0], acc)
+    acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[1], b_frag[1], acc)
+    O[lane] = acc
+
 
+@substrate.jit
+def _probe_frag_accum(
+    A: S.Tensor((64, 4), S.u32),
+    B: S.Tensor((64, 4), S.u32),
+    O: S.Tensor((64, 16), S.f32),
+):
+    lane = S.thread_id(0)
+    a_frag = S.view(A[lane], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+    b_frag = S.view(B[lane], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+    acc = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+    acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[0], b_frag[0], acc)
+    acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[1], b_frag[1], acc)
+    O[lane] = acc
+
+
 class ModelNew(nn.Module):
     def __init__(self):
         super().__init__()
+        self._shape = (M, K, N)
+        self._launch = None
+        self._cached_ptrs = None
+
+    def _get_launch(self, A, B):
+        a_ptr = A.untyped_storage().data_ptr()
+        b_ptr = B.untyped_storage().data_ptr()
+        ptrs = (a_ptr, b_ptr)
+        if self._launch is None or self._cached_ptrs != ptrs:
+            self._cached_ptrs = ptrs
+            self._launch = gemm_kernel_mfma[lambda: ((N // BLOCK_N, M // BLOCK_M, 1), (THREADS_PER_BLOCK, 1, 1))]
+        return self._launch
 
     def forward(self, A, B):

-            return torch.matmul(A, B)
         A = A.contiguous()
         B = B.contiguous()
-        C = torch.empty((32768, 32768), device=A.device, dtype=A.dtype)
-        gemm_kernel[lambda: ((1, 1, 1), (1, 1, 1))](A, B, C)
+        C = torch.empty((M, N), device=A.device, dtype=A.dtype)
+        launch = self._get_launch(A, B)
+        launch(
+            A,
+            B,
+            C,
+            A.numel() * A.element_size(),
+            B.numel() * B.element_size(),
+        )
         return C

+    warp_row = warp // 2
+    warp_col = warp % 2
+
+    block_row = S.block_id(1) * BLOCK_M
+    block_col = S.block_id(0) * BLOCK_N
+
+    shared_a = S.make_shared((BLOCK_M, K), S.bf16)
+    shared_b = S.make_shared((K, BLOCK_N), S.bf16)
+
+    a_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(A, a_range_bytes)
+    b_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(B, b_range_bytes)
+
+    zero = S.convert(0, S.i32)
+
+    a_linear = tid * 8
+    a_row = a_linear // K
+    a_col = a_linear % K
+    a_offset = ((block_row + a_row) * K + a_col) * BF16_BYTES
+    a_pack = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(a_rsrc, zero, S.convert(a_offset, S.i32), 0)
+    a_vals = S.view(a_pack, S.Tensor((8,), S.bf16))
+    for i in S.range(8):
+        shared_a[a_row, a_col + i] = a_vals[i]
+
+    b_linear = tid * 8
+    b_row = b_linear // BLOCK_N
+    b_col = b_linear % BLOCK_N
+    b_offset = (b_row * N + block_col + b_col) * BF16_BYTES
+    b_pack = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(b_rsrc, zero, S.convert(b_offset, S.i32), 0)
+    b_vals = S.view(b_pack, S.Tensor((8,), S.bf16))
+    for i in S.range(8):
+        shared_b[b_row, b_col + i] = b_vals[i]
+
+    S.syncthreads()
+
+    acc = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+    wave_row = warp_row * 32
+    wave_col = warp_col * 32
+    lane_row = lane % 32
+    lane_col = lane % 32
+    lane_k8 = (lane // 32) * 8
+
+    for phase in S.range(2):
+        a_frag_words = S.full((8,), S.convert(0.0, S.bf16), S.bf16)
+        b_frag_words = S.full((8,), S.convert(0.0, S.bf16), S.bf16)
+        phase_k = phase * 16 + lane_k8
+        for i in S.range(8):
+            a_frag_words[i] = shared_a[wave_row + lane_row, phase_k + i]
+            b_frag_words[i] = shared_b[phase_k + i, wave_col + lane_col]
+
+        a_frag = S.view(a_frag_words, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+        b_frag = S.view(b_frag_words, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+        acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[0], b_frag[0], acc)
+        acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[1], b_frag[1], acc)
+
+    out_col = block_col + wave_col + lane_col
+    row_group = (lane // 32) * 4
+    for i in S.range(16):
+        out_row = block_row + wave_row + (i // 4) * 8 + row_group + (i % 4)
+        C[out_row, out_col] = S.convert(acc[i], S.bf16)
+
+
+@substrate.jit
+def _probe_wave_accum(
+    A: S.Tensor((32, 16), S.bf16),
+    B: S.Tensor((16, 32), S.bf16),
+    O: S.Tensor((64, 16), S.f32),
+    a_range_bytes: S.i32,
+    b_range_bytes: S.i32,
 ):
-    for i in S.range(M):
-        for j in S.range(N):
-            acc = S.convert(0.0, S.f32)
-            for kk in S.range(K):
-                acc += S.convert(A[i, kk], S.f32) * S.convert(B[kk, j], S.f32)
-            C[i, j] = S.convert(acc, S.bf16)
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    lane = tid
+    zero = S.convert(0, S.i32)
 
+    a_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(A, a_range_bytes)
+    b_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(B, b_range_bytes)
+
+    a_offset = tid * 16
+    b_offset = tid * 16
+    a_pack = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(a_rsrc, zero, S.convert(a_offset, S.i32), 0)
+    b_pack = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(b_rsrc, zero, S.convert(b_offset, S.i32), 0)
+    a_frag = S.view(a_pack, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+    b_frag = S.view(b_pack, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+    acc = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+    acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[0], b_frag[0], acc)
+    acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[1], b_frag[1], acc)
+    O[lane] = acc
+
 
+@substrate.jit
+def _probe_frag_accum(
+    A: S.Tensor((64, 4), S.u32),
+    B: S.Tensor((64, 4), S.u32),
+    O: S.Tensor((64, 16), S.f32),
+):
+    lane = S.thread_id(0)
+    a_frag = S.view(A[lane], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+    b_frag = S.view(B[lane], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+    acc = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+    acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[0], b_frag[0], acc)
+    acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[1], b_frag[1], acc)
+    O[lane] = acc
+
+
 class ModelNew(nn.Module):
     def __init__(self):
         super().__init__()
+        self._shape = (M, K, N)
+        self._launch = None
+        self._cached_ptrs = None
+
+    def _get_launch(self, A, B):
+        a_ptr = A.untyped_storage().data_ptr()
+        b_ptr = B.untyped_storage().data_ptr()
+        ptrs = (a_ptr, b_ptr)
+        if self._launch is None or self._cached_ptrs != ptrs:
+            self._cached_ptrs = ptrs
+            self._launch = gemm_kernel_mfma[lambda: ((N // BLOCK_N, M // BLOCK_M, 1), (THREADS_PER_BLOCK, 1, 1))]
+        return self._launch
 
     def forward(self, A, B):
-        if tuple(A.shape) != (32768, 32) or tuple(B.shape) != (32, 32768):
-            return torch.matmul(A, B)
         A = A.contiguous()
         B = B.contiguous()
-        C = torch.empty((32768, 32768), device=A.device, dtype=A.dtype)
-        gemm_kernel[lambda: ((1, 1, 1), (1, 1, 1))](A, B, C)
+        C = torch.empty((M, N), device=A.device, dtype=A.dtype)
+        launch = self._get_launch(A, B)
+        launch(
+            A,
+            B,
+            C,
+            A.numel() * A.element_size(),
+            B.numel() * B.element_size(),
+        )
         return C

codex
The remaining compile blocker is specifically the private bf16 fragment buffer construction, not the MFMA mapping anymore. I’m making one focused API-level adjustment there before changing the data path again.

+    warp = tid // WAVE_SIZE
+    warp_row = warp // 2
+    warp_col = warp % 2

+    block_col = S.block_id(0) * BLOCK_N

+    shared_b = S.make_shared((K, BLOCK_N), S.bf16)

+    a_vals = S.view(a_pack, S.Tensor((8,), S.bf16))

+        out_row = block_row + wave_row + (i // 4) * 8 + row_group + (i % 4)
+        C[out_row, out_col] = S.convert(acc[i], S.bf16)
+

+@substrate.jit
+def _probe_wave_accum(
+    A: S.Tensor((32, 16), S.bf16),
+    B: S.Tensor((16, 32), S.bf16),
+    O: S.Tensor((64, 16), S.f32),
+    a_range_bytes: S.i32,
+    b_range_bytes: S.i32,

-    for i in S.range(M):
-        for j in S.range(N):

-            for kk in S.range(K):
-                acc += S.convert(A[i, kk], S.f32) * S.convert(B[kk, j], S.f32)
-            C[i, j] = S.convert(acc, S.bf16)

+    lane = tid
+    zero = S.convert(0, S.i32)
 
+    a_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(A, a_range_bytes)
+    b_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(B, b_range_bytes)
+
+    a_offset = tid * 16
+    b_offset = tid * 16
+    a_pack = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(a_rsrc, zero, S.convert(a_offset, S.i32), 0)
+    b_pack = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(b_rsrc, zero, S.convert(b_offset, S.i32), 0)
+    a_frag = S.view(a_pack, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+    b_frag = S.view(b_pack, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+    acc = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+    acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[0], b_frag[0], acc)
+    acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[1], b_frag[1], acc)
+    O[lane] = acc
+
 
+@substrate.jit
+def _probe_frag_accum(
+    A: S.Tensor((64, 4), S.u32),
+    B: S.Tensor((64, 4), S.u32),
+    O: S.Tensor((64, 16), S.f32),
+):
+    lane = S.thread_id(0)
+    a_frag = S.view(A[lane], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))

+    O[lane] = acc
+
+
 class ModelNew(nn.Module):
     def __init__(self):
         super().__init__()
+        self._shape = (M, K, N)
+        self._launch = None
+        self._cached_ptrs = None
+
+    def _get_launch(self, A, B):
+        a_ptr = A.untyped_storage().data_ptr()
+        b_ptr = B.untyped_storage().data_ptr()

+        if self._launch is None or self._cached_ptrs != ptrs:
+            self._cached_ptrs = ptrs
+            self._launch = gemm_kernel_mfma[lambda: ((N // BLOCK_N, M // BLOCK_M, 1), (THREADS_PER_BLOCK, 1, 1))]

     def forward(self, A, B):

         B = B.contiguous()

+            B,

+            A.numel() * A.element_size(),
+            B.numel() * B.element_size(),
+        )

codex
I have one last low-risk backend workaround to try: move the per-thread bf16 fragment buffer from private memory into a thread-owned row inside LDS, then `view` that full row directly. That avoids both the unsupported private bf16 path and the shared subview lowering path that failed earlier.
apply patch
patch: completed

+def gemm_kernel_mfma(

+    a_range_bytes: S.i32,
+    b_range_bytes: S.i32,
+):
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    lane = tid % WAVE_SIZE
+    warp = tid // WAVE_SIZE
+    warp_row = warp // 2
+    warp_col = warp % 2
+
+    block_row = S.block_id(1) * BLOCK_M
+    block_col = S.block_id(0) * BLOCK_N
+
+    shared_a = S.make_shared((BLOCK_M, K), S.bf16)
+    shared_b = S.make_shared((K, BLOCK_N), S.bf16)
+    scratch_a = S.make_shared((THREADS_PER_BLOCK, 8), S.bf16)
+    scratch_b = S.make_shared((THREADS_PER_BLOCK, 8), S.bf16)
+
+    a_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(A, a_range_bytes)
+    b_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(B, b_range_bytes)
+

+
+    a_linear = tid * 8
+    a_row = a_linear // K
+    a_col = a_linear % K
+    a_offset = ((block_row + a_row) * K + a_col) * BF16_BYTES
+    a_pack = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(a_rsrc, zero, S.convert(a_offset, S.i32), 0)
+    a_vals = S.view(a_pack, S.Tensor((8,), S.bf16))
+    for i in S.range(8):
+        shared_a[a_row, a_col + i] = a_vals[i]
+
+    b_linear = tid * 8
+    b_row = b_linear // BLOCK_N
+    b_col = b_linear % BLOCK_N
+    b_offset = (b_row * N + block_col + b_col) * BF16_BYTES
+    b_pack = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(b_rsrc, zero, S.convert(b_offset, S.i32), 0)
+    b_vals = S.view(b_pack, S.Tensor((8,), S.bf16))

+
+    for phase in S.range(2):

+
+        a_frag = S.view(scratch_a[tid], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+        b_frag = S.view(scratch_b[tid], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
